**Summary of `README.md`**

The repository contains *Consoul*, an AIpowered terminal assistant. It offers a rich TUI, a simple CLI, and a Python SDK for interacting with various LLM providers (Claude, GPT4, Gemini, Ollama, etc.). Core features include:

* Interactive AI chat with streaming responses.
* File editing, code search, and image analysis tools.
* Multiprovider support and localmodel execution.
* Detailed documentation and quickstart guides.
* Strong security controls: permission policies, approval workflows, audit logs.
